27-30 and 24-26 Match Point Decklists
=====================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 24, 2019 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











One player finished with 30 points (10-0) in the Standard portion of the 2019 Mythic Championship I, three players finished with 27 points (9-1), two players finished with 25 points (8-1-1) and twenty players finished with 24 points (8-2).


30 POINTS (10-0) OR 27 POINTS (9-1)
===================================







#### Hamilton, Michael - Esper Control


#####
